//===== TERMUXFILE: scripts/build_runner.sh =====
#!/data/data/com.termux/files/usr/bin/bash
#
# build_runner.sh — Autonomous-safe version
#
# Build status contract:
#   /sdcard/ai-automation/build_status.txt    → "SUCCESS" or "FAILURE"
#   /sdcard/ai-automation/build_complete.flag → touched last, always
#
# Android reads build_status.txt for result. Folder existence never used.

set -euo pipefail

REPO_DIR="/data/data/com.termux/files/home/jarvis"
BASE_DIR="/sdcard/ai-automation"
AI_OUTPUT="$BASE_DIR/ai-output.txt"
DOWNLOAD_DIR="/sdcard/Download"
COMPLETE_FLAG="$BASE_DIR/build_complete.flag"
ASSEMBLED_FLAG="$BASE_DIR/downloads_assembled.flag"
SNAPSHOT_FILE="$BASE_DIR/download_snapshot.txt"
STATUS_FILE="$BASE_DIR/build_status.txt"
LOG_DIR="$BASE_DIR/logs"
ERROR_LOG_DIR="$BASE_DIR/build_error_logs"

mkdir -p "$LOG_DIR"
exec >> "$LOG_DIR/build_runner.log" 2>&1

echo ""
echo "=== build_runner.sh START $(date) args=${*:-none} ==="

# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
# MODE: snapshot
# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
if [[ "${1:-}" == "--snapshot" ]]; then
    echo "[snapshot] Recording existing files"
    rm -f "$SNAPSHOT_FILE"
    find "$DOWNLOAD_DIR" -maxdepth 1 -type f -exec basename {} \; \
        > "$SNAPSHOT_FILE" 2>/dev/null || true
    echo "[snapshot] Done"
    exit 0
fi

# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
# MODE: assemble downloaded files
# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
if [[ "${1:-}" == "--assemble-downloads" ]]; then
    echo "[assemble] Starting"

    declare -A BEFORE
    if [[ -f "$SNAPSHOT_FILE" ]]; then
        while IFS= read -r name; do
            BEFORE["$name"]=1
        done < "$SNAPSHOT_FILE"
    fi

    CODE_EXTS="kt java py txt xml json gradle kts sh cpp c h ts js md"
    NEW_FILES=()
    DEADLINE=$(( $(date +%s) + 30 ))

    while (( $(date +%s) < DEADLINE )); do
        while IFS= read -r -d '' f; do
            NAME=$(basename "$f")
            EXT="${NAME##*.}"
            if [[ -z "${BEFORE[$NAME]+_}" ]] && \
               [[ -s "$f" ]] && \
               echo "$CODE_EXTS" | grep -qw "$EXT"; then
                NEW_FILES+=("$f")
            fi
        done < <(find "$DOWNLOAD_DIR" -maxdepth 1 -type f -print0 2>/dev/null)
        [[ ${#NEW_FILES[@]} -gt 0 ]] && break
        sleep 1
    done

    if [[ ${#NEW_FILES[@]} -eq 0 ]]; then
        echo "[assemble] ERROR: No new files"
        exit 1
    fi

    > "$AI_OUTPUT"
    for f in "${NEW_FILES[@]}"; do
        NAME=$(basename "$f")
        printf '//===== FILE: %s =====\n' "$NAME" >> "$AI_OUTPUT"
        cat "$f" >> "$AI_OUTPUT"
        printf '\n\n' >> "$AI_OUTPUT"
    done

    touch "$ASSEMBLED_FLAG"
    rm -f "$SNAPSHOT_FILE"
    echo "[assemble] DONE"
    exit 0
fi

# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
# MODE: normal build
# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

# Stale state cleanup — always before a new build
echo "[cleanup] Removing stale flags and error logs"
rm -f "$COMPLETE_FLAG"
rm -f "$STATUS_FILE"
rm -rf "$ERROR_LOG_DIR"
mkdir -p "$ERROR_LOG_DIR"

echo "[normal] Starting build mode"
cd "$REPO_DIR"

# Clean old error logs from repo before reset to prevent re-detection
echo "[cleanup] Removing old build_error_logs from repo"
rm -rf "$REPO_DIR/build_error_logs"

echo "[sync] Force syncing with origin/main"
git fetch origin main
git reset --hard origin/main
echo "[sync] Repo synced"

echo "[copy] Updating ai-output.txt"
cp "$AI_OUTPUT" "$REPO_DIR/ai-output.txt"

git config user.name  "AutoBuild Bot"
git config user.email "bot@autobuild.local"

git add ai-output.txt
git commit -m "AutoBuild: update ai-output.txt" || echo "[skip] Nothing to commit"
git push origin main || echo "[warn] git push failed"

echo "[wait] Waiting 20s for workflows to queue..."
sleep 20

# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
# Watch APK workflow
# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
APK_WORKFLOW_NAME="Build APK"
CONCLUSION=""

echo "[watch] Looking for APK workflow run..."
APK_RUN_ID=$(gh run list \
    --workflow="$APK_WORKFLOW_NAME" \
    --limit=1 \
    --json databaseId \
    -q '.[0].databaseId' 2>/dev/null || true)

if [[ -z "${APK_RUN_ID:-}" ]]; then
    echo "[warn] No APK workflow run found — writing FAILURE"
    echo "FAILURE" > "$STATUS_FILE"
    touch "$COMPLETE_FLAG"
    echo "=== build_runner.sh DONE (no run found) $(date) ==="
    exit 0
fi

echo "[watch] Watching run $APK_RUN_ID..."
gh run watch "$APK_RUN_ID" --exit-status || true

# Deterministic result via gh run view
echo "[status] Querying conclusion for run $APK_RUN_ID..."
CONCLUSION=$(gh run view "$APK_RUN_ID" \
    --json conclusion \
    -q '.conclusion' 2>/dev/null || echo "unknown")
echo "[status] Conclusion = $CONCLUSION"

# Final sync to fetch any committed error logs
echo "[sync] Final git pull"
git fetch origin main
git reset --hard origin/main

# Write build_status.txt and handle logs
if [[ "$CONCLUSION" == "success" ]]; then
    echo "[result] BUILD SUCCESS"
    echo "SUCCESS" > "$STATUS_FILE"
    rm -rf "$ERROR_LOG_DIR"
    mkdir -p "$ERROR_LOG_DIR"
    echo "[result] Cleared error logs from shared storage"
else
    echo "[result] BUILD FAILURE (conclusion=$CONCLUSION)"
    echo "FAILURE" > "$STATUS_FILE"

    if [[ -d "$REPO_DIR/build_error_logs" ]] && \
       [[ -f "$REPO_DIR/build_error_logs/error_summary.txt" ]]; then
        rm -rf "$ERROR_LOG_DIR"
        mkdir -p "$ERROR_LOG_DIR"
        cp -f "$REPO_DIR/build_error_logs/"* "$ERROR_LOG_DIR/" 2>/dev/null || true
        echo "[result] Error logs copied to $ERROR_LOG_DIR"
    else
        echo "[warn] FAILURE but no error_summary.txt found in repo"
        mkdir -p "$ERROR_LOG_DIR"
        echo "Build failed but no error_summary.txt was committed." \
            > "$ERROR_LOG_DIR/error_summary.txt"
        echo "(gh conclusion=$CONCLUSION, no log files found)" \
            >> "$ERROR_LOG_DIR/error_summary.txt"
    fi
fi

# Always touch build_complete.flag last
echo "[final] Touching build_complete.flag"
touch "$COMPLETE_FLAG" || true

echo "=== build_runner.sh DONE (conclusion=$CONCLUSION) $(date) ==="


//===== TERMUXFILE: workflows/Ai-codegen.yml =====
name: AI Code Generator

on:
  workflow_dispatch:
  push:
    paths:
      - ai-output.txt

permissions:
  contents: write

jobs:
  generate:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest

    steps:
      - name: Checkout repo
        uses: actions/checkout@v4
        with:
          fetch-depth: 0

      - name: Set up Python (GitHub runner only)
        if: ${{ !env.ACT }}
        uses: actions/setup-python@v5
        with:
          python-version: "3.11"

      - name: Use system Python (Termux / act)
        if: ${{ env.ACT }}
        run: |
          echo "Using Termux Python"
          python --version

      - name: Run AI Code Generator
        run: |
          python ai-code.py ~/storage/shared/Download/ai-output.txt

      - name: Clean act cache (local only)
        if: ${{ env.ACT }}
        run: |
          echo "Cleaning act cache..."
          rm -rf ~/.cache/act || true


//===== TERMUXFILE: workflows/jarvis_start.sh =====
#!/data/data/com.termux/files/usr/bin/bash
# ================================================================
#  jarvis_start.sh  —  Minimal Phone A startup
#  Only starts what is essential for the A→B agent loop:
#    1. ADB connect Phone A + Phone B
#    2. Verify Phone B Claude bridge is reachable
#
#  Phone A : 192.168.29.48:37891
#  Phone B : 192.168.29.110:45999  (Claude brain)
#
#  Usage:
#    bash ~/workflows/jarvis_start.sh
#    bash ~/workflows/jarvis_start.sh --stop
# ================================================================

PHONE_A="192.168.29.48:37891"
PHONE_B="192.168.29.110:45999"
PHONE_B_BRIDGE="http://192.168.29.110:8890"

GREEN="\033[0;32m"; YELLOW="\033[1;33m"; RED="\033[0;31m"; NC="\033[0m"
log()  { echo -e "${GREEN}[jarvis]${NC} $*"; }
warn() { echo -e "${YELLOW}[jarvis]${NC} $*"; }
err()  { echo -e "${RED}[jarvis]${NC} $*"; }

# ── Stop mode ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
if [ "$1" = "--stop" ]; then
    log "Disconnecting ADB devices..."
    adb disconnect "$PHONE_A" 2>/dev/null && log "  ✓ Phone A disconnected" || true
    adb disconnect "$PHONE_B" 2>/dev/null && log "  ✓ Phone B disconnected" || true
    log "Done."; exit 0
fi

echo ""
echo "╔══════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗"
echo "║   JARVIS START  —  Agent Loop (A → B)               ║"
echo "╚══════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝"
echo ""

# ── 1. ADB connect ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
log "Connecting ADB devices..."

adb connect "$PHONE_A" 2>&1 | grep -q "connected" \
    && log "  ✓ Phone A ($PHONE_A)" \
    || warn "  ✗ Phone A failed — screencap will fail"

adb connect "$PHONE_B" 2>&1 | grep -q "connected" \
    && log "  ✓ Phone B ($PHONE_B)" \
    || warn "  ✗ Phone B failed — bridge unreachable"

# ── 2. Verify Phone B bridge ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
log "Checking Phone B Claude bridge..."
HEALTH=$(curl -sf --max-time 5 "$PHONE_B_BRIDGE/health")
if [ $? -eq 0 ]; then
    log "  ✓ Bridge online — Claude brain ACTIVE"
    log "  $HEALTH"
else
    err "  ✗ Bridge offline!"
    err "  On Phone B run: python3 ~/claude_bridge.py"
    echo ""
    exit 1
fi

# ── 3. Quick A→B smoke test ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
log "Running A→B smoke test..."
RESULT=$(curl -sf --max-time 30 -X POST "$PHONE_B_BRIDGE/chat" \
    -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
    -d '{"prompt": "Reply with only the word: ready"}')
if echo "$RESULT" | grep -q '"success":true'; then
    log "  ✓ A→B round-trip OK"
    log "  Response: $RESULT"
else
    warn "  ✗ Smoke test failed or timed out"
    warn "  Raw: $RESULT"
fi

# ── Summary ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
echo ""
echo "╔══════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗"
echo "║   READY                                              ║"
echo "╚══════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝"
echo ""
log "Phone A (agent)  : $PHONE_A"
log "Phone B (brain)  : $PHONE_B_BRIDGE"
echo ""
log "Run agent:"
log "  cd ~/workflows"
log "  python3 test/jarvis-agent/agent/controller.py --task 'Open WhatsApp' --device '$PHONE_A'"
echo ""
